{"type":"tool_use","timestamp":1781034472199,"sessionID":"ses_1521418c2ffe0nddbrJpdqlOSY","part":{"type":"tool","tool":"write","callID":"call_00_GneERb3FBTpoQ8wKLOVm8257","state":{"status":"completed","input":{"filePath":"/app/analyze2.py","content":"import pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom pathlib import Path\nimport json\n\nbase = Path('/app')\n\n# Load data\nusers = pd.read_csv(base / 'user_001.csv')\nlisting_files = sorted(base.glob('listing_*.csv'))\nlistings = pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f) for f in listing_files], ignore_index=True)\npurchases = pd.read_csv(base / 'purchase_001.csv')\ncategories = pd.read_csv(base / 'category_001.csv')\n\n# Merge purchases with listings -> category_id\npurchases_with_cat = purchases.merge(listings[['listing_id', 'category_id']], on='listing_id', how='left')\npurchases_with_cat = purchases_with_cat.merge(categories[['category_id', 'category_name']], on='category_id', how='left')\npurchases_with_cat = purchases_with_cat.merge(users[['user_id', 'city', 'user_type']], left_on='buyer_id', right_on='user_id', how='left')\n\n# Cities with non-negligible users (>= 50)\ncity_user_counts = users.groupby('city').size()\nsignificant_cities = city_user_counts[city_user_counts >= 50].index.tolist()\nprint(f\"Significant cities ({len(significant_cities)}): {significant_cities}\")\n\n# Filter data to significant cities\nusers_sig = users[users['city'].isin(significant_cities)].copy()\npurchases_sig = purchases_with_cat[purchases_with_cat['city'].isin(significant_cities)].copy()\n\n# Users per city\ncity_users = users_sig.groupby('city').size().to_dict()\n\n# --- Approach: User-type normalized ---\n# For each user_type, compute global purchase rate per category\nglobal_type_cat = purchases_sig.groupby(['user_type', 'category_name']).size().reset_index(name='type_cat_purchases')\nuser_type_total = users_sig.groupby('user_type').size().reset_index(name='type_total')\nglobal_type_cat = global_type_cat.merge(user_type_total, on='user_type')\nglobal_type_cat['rate'] = global_type_cat['type_cat_purchases'] / global_type_cat['type_total']\n\n# City user type composition\ncity_type_dist = users_sig.groupby(['city', 'user_type']).size().reset_index(name='type_count')\n\n# Compute expected purchases for each (city, category)\n# expected = sum over user_types of (type_count_in_city * global_rate_for_type)\nrows = []\nfor city in significant_cities:\n    city_types = city_type_dist[city_type_dist['city'] == city]\n    for cat in categories['category_name']:\n        expected = 0.0\n        for _, tr in city_types.iterrows():\n            ut = tr['user_type']\n            tc = tr['type_count']\n            match = global_type_cat[(global_type_cat['user_type'] == ut) & (global_type_cat['category_name'] == cat)]\n            if len(match) > 0:\n                expected += tc * match['rate'].values[0]\n        rows.append({'city': city, 'category_name': cat, 'expected': expected})\n\nexpected_df = pd.DataFrame(rows)\n\n# Actual purchases per (city, category)\nactual_df = purchases_sig.groupby(['city', 'category_name']).size().reset_index(name='actual')\n\n# Merge\nmerged = expected_df.merge(actual_df, on=['city', 'category_name'], how='left')\nmerged['actual'] = sorted(base.glob('listing_*.csv'))\nlistings = pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f) for f in listing_files], ignore_index=True)\npurchases = pd.read_csv(base / 'purchase_001.csv')\ncategories = pd.read_csv(base / 'category_001.csv')\n\n# Merge purchases with listings and categories\npurchases_with_cat = purchases.merge(listings[['listing_id', 'category_id']], on='listing_id', how='left')\npurchases_with_cat = purchases_with_cat.merge(categories[['category_id', 'category_name']], on='category_id', how='left')\npurchases_with_cat = purchases_with_cat.merge(users[['user_id', 'city', 'user_type']], left_on='buyer_id', right_on='user_id', how='left')\n\n# Significant cities: >= 50 users\ncity_user_counts = users.groupby('city').size()\nsignificant_cities = city_user_counts[city_user_counts >= 50].index.tolist()\nsignificant_cities.sort()\n\nusers_sig = users[users['city'].isin(significant_cities)].copy()\npurchases_sig = purchases_with_cat[purchases_with_cat['city'].isin(significant_cities)].copy()\ncity_users = users_sig.groupby('city').size().to_dict()\n\n# Only popular categories (>= 100 global purchases)\ncat_pop = purchases_sig.groupby('category_name').size()\npopular_cats = cat_pop[cat_pop >= 100].index.tolist()\n\n# === APPROACH A: User-type normalized ratio ===\n# Global purchase rate per user_type per category\nglobal_type_cat = purchases_sig.groupby(['user_type', 'category_name']).size().reset_index(name='purchases')\nuser_type_totals = users_sig.groupby('user_type').size().reset_index(name='total_users')\nglobal_type_cat = global_type_cat.merge(user_type_totals, on='user_type')\nglobal_type_cat['rate'] = global_type_cat['purchases'] / global_type_cat['total_users']\n\n# City user type composition\ncity_type_dist = users_sig.groupby(['city', 'user_type']).size().reset_index(name='count')\n\n# Expected purchases per (city, category)\nrows = []\nfor city in significant_cities:\n    city_types = city_type_dist[city_type_dist['city'] == city]\n    for cat in categories['category_name']:\n        expected = 0.0\n        for _, tr in city_types.iterrows():\n            match = global_type_cat[(global_type_cat['user_type'] == tr['user_type']) & \n                                    (global_type_cat['category_name'] == cat)]\n            if len(match) > 0:\n                expected += tr['count'] * match['rate'].values[0]\n        rows.append({'city': city, 'category_name': cat, 'expected': expected})\n\nexpected_df = pd.DataFrame(rows)\n\n# Actual purchases\nactual_df = purchases_sig.groupby(['city', 'category_name']).size().reset_index(name='actual')\n\n# Compare\nmerged = expected_df.merge(actual_df, on=['city', 'category_name'], how='left')\nmerged['actual'] = merged['actual'].fillna(0)\nmerged['ratio'] = merged['actual'] / merged['expected'].replace(0, np.nan)\n\n# Filter: popular categories, expected >= 5\nmerged_f = merged[(merged['category_name'].isin(popular_cats)) & (merged['expected'] >= 5)].copy()\n\n# Approach A: ratio < 0.4\napproach_a = {}\nfor _, row in merged_f.iterrows():\n    if row['ratio'] < 0.4:\n        city = row['city']\n        if city not in approach_a:\n            approach_a[city] = set()\n        approach_a[city].add(row['category_name'])\n\n# === APPROACH B: Binomial test ===\ntotal_users_sig = len(users_sig)\napproach_b = {}\nfor cat in popular_cats:\n    cat_global = purchases_sig[purchases_sig['category_name'] == cat]['category_name'].count()\n    global_prob = cat_global / total_users_sig\n    if global_prob == 0:\n        continue\n    \n    for city in significant_cities:\n        n = city_users[city]\n        expected_global = n * global_prob\n        if expected_global < 3:\n            continue\n        \n        actual_row = actual_df[(actual_df['city'] == city) & (actual_df['category_name'] == cat)]\n        actual = actual_row['actual'].values[0] if len(actual_row) > 0 else 0\n        \n        p_value = stats.binom.cdf(actual, n, global_prob)\n        \n        if p_value < 0.01 and actual < expected_global:\n            if city not in approach_b:\n                approach_b[city] = set()\n            approach_b[city].add(cat)\n\n# Combined: intersection of both approaches\ncombined = {}\nall_cities = set(list(approach_a.keys()) + list(approach_b.keys()))\nfor city in all_cities:\n    cats_a = approach_a.get(city, set())\n    cats_b = approach_b.get(city, set())\n    intersect = cats_a & cats_b\n    if intersect:\n        combined[city] = sorted(intersect)\n\n# Build final answer: sorted by city\nfinal_answer = {city: sorted(cats) for city, cats in sorted(combined.items())}\n\n# Write to answer.json\nwith open(base / 'answer.json', 'w') as f:\n    json.dump(final_answer, f, indent=2)\n\nprint(f\"Answer written to /app/answer.json\")\nprint(json.dumps(final_answer,
